üì¢ Calling all cutting-edge IT projects!

ü§î What is Everscale Grants?
Everscale Grants is a program of the Everscale DeFi Alliance that is looking to bring in promising IT projects capable of contributing to the growth of the Everscale ecosystem.

üí∏ Projects that are selected for the grants program will recieve:

üíé Financial support for building an MVP and/or achieving an important development milestone

üíé Technical guidance and support from industry experts

üíé Project structuring and market support

üë®‚Äçüíª Some pointers for those looking to apply:

üíé Be as detailed as possible! Let us know everything and then some about your project! The more we know the better we will able to determine whether your project is the right fit for us

üíé Provide personal contact information in your application so we can contact you if we have additional questions or want further clarifications

üíé Don't spam us with multiple applications. We will only consider one application per project.
